## Instruction

I have prepared two data tables in the Notion `Oil Price` page. Please fetch WTI and Brent monthly prices for the last 12 months from Yahoo Finance, analyze the WTI-Brent oil spread changes and calculate related indicators, implement a z-score-based spread trading strategy backtest, and return a summary report.

For detailed technical specifications, please refer to the `detail.md` file.

<Accordion title="full return">
```json
- **Data**: Fetch monthly data for WTI (CL=F) and Brent (BZ=F) from Yahoo Finance for the last 12 complete calendar months. Prices should be rounded to 4 decimal places, percentages to 2 decimal places.
- **Calculations**:

  | Indicator        | Description                                                                                                                                |
  | ---------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
  | Brent-WTI Spread | Brent Close - WTI Close                                                                                                                    |
  | MoM%             | (Current Month / Previous Month - 1) √ó 100%                                                                                                |
  | Z-Score(6m)      | Standardized using mean and SAMPLE standard deviation (ddof=1) of the last 6 spreads (z=0 when sample < 4 or std = 0, clipped to [-3,3]).  |

- **Backtest Strategy**: Generate signals based on z-score (z ‚â§ -1: long spread = long Brent + short WTI; z ‚â• +1: short spread = short Brent + long WTI; otherwise flat). Signals generated at month-end, held for 1 month, closed at next month-end. Only one position at a time; equal weight for both legs; 0.40% round-trip cost included in monthly net returns. Calculate total return, annualized return, Sharpe ratio, win rate, and maximum drawdown.

  - **Tip:** Entry Month refers to signal generation month, Exit Month refers to position closing month. Position returns are calculated from signal generation month to position closing month (spanning 2 calendar months)

- **Write results to** **`Oil Market Summary`** **Oil Market Summary** and **`Spread Strategy Backtest`** **Spread Strategy Backtest** data tables. For `Spread Strategy Backtest`, update the unique "Metric" row and add/update corresponding "Trade" rows for each executed trade:

  - When Type=Metric: fill in `Period Start`, `Period End`, `Trades`, `Total Return %`, `Annualized Return %`, `Sharpe (ann.)`, `Win Rate %`, `Max Drawdown %`, `Cost Assumption`;
  - When Type=Trade: fill in `Entry Month`, `Exit Month`, `Signal`, `Entry Spread`, `Exit Spread`, `Leg Returns %`, `Net PnL %`, `Notes`.

```
</Accordion>

<div className="tool-call-box">
<svg width="14px" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M13.0164 2C10.8193 2 9.03825 3.72453 9.03825 5.85185V8.51852H15.9235V9.25926H5.97814C3.78107 9.25926 2 10.9838 2 13.1111L2 18.8889C2 21.0162 3.78107 22.7407 5.97814 22.7407H8.27322V19.4815C8.27322 17.3542 10.0543 15.6296 12.2514 15.6296H19.5956C21.4547 15.6296 22.9617 14.1704 22.9617 12.3704V5.85185C22.9617 3.72453 21.1807 2 18.9836 2H13.0164ZM12.0984 6.74074C12.8589 6.74074 13.4754 6.14378 13.4754 5.40741C13.4754 4.67103 12.8589 4.07407 12.0984 4.07407C11.3378 4.07407 10.7213 4.67103 10.7213 5.40741C10.7213 6.14378 11.3378 6.74074 12.0984 6.74074Z" fill="#327EBD"/><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M18.9834 30C21.1805 30 22.9616 28.2755 22.9616 26.1482V23.4815L16.0763 23.4815L16.0763 22.7408L26.0217 22.7408C28.2188 22.7408 29.9998 21.0162 29.9998 18.8889V13.1111C29.9998 10.9838 28.2188 9.25928 26.0217 9.25928L23.7266 9.25928V12.5185C23.7266 14.6459 21.9455 16.3704 19.7485 16.3704L12.4042 16.3704C10.5451 16.3704 9.03809 17.8296 9.03809 19.6296L9.03809 26.1482C9.03809 28.2755 10.8192 30 13.0162 30H18.9834ZM19.9015 25.2593C19.1409 25.2593 18.5244 25.8562 18.5244 26.5926C18.5244 27.329 19.1409 27.9259 19.9015 27.9259C20.662 27.9259 21.2785 27.329 21.2785 26.5926C21.2785 25.8562 20.662 25.2593 19.9015 25.2593Z" fill="#FFDA4B"/></svg> `python-execute`

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get the last 12 complete calendar months
today = datetime.now()
# Get the first day of current month, then go back 12 months
start_of_current_month = today.replace(day=1)
end_date = start_of_current_month - timedelta(days=1)  # Last day of previous month
start_date = (end_date.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11)).replace(day=1)  # 12 months back

print(f"Fetching data from {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch WTI (CL=F) and Brent (BZ=F) data
wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=start_date, end=end_date + timedelta(days=1), interval='1d')
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=start_date, end=end_date + timedelta(days=1), interval='1d')

print(f"WTI data shape: {wti.shape}")
print(f"Brent data shape: {brent.shape}")

# Get monthly data (last trading day of each month)
wti_monthly = wti.resample('M').last()
brent_monthly = brent.resample('M').last()

print(f"WTI monthly data shape: {wti_monthly.shape}")
print(f"Brent monthly data shape: {brent_monthly.shape}")

# Display the data
print("\nWTI Monthly Prices:")
print(wti_monthly[['Close']].head(10))

print("\nBrent Monthly Prices:")
print(brent_monthly[['Close']].head(10))
```
</div>

```python 
# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_monthly.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_monthly['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_monthly['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get the last 12 complete calendar months
today = datetime.now()
start_of_current_month = today.replace(day=1)
end_date = start_of_current_month - timedelta(days=1)
start_date = (end_date.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11)).replace(day=1)

print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data
wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=start_date, end=end_date + timedelta(days=1), interval='1d', progress=False)
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=start_date, end=end_date + timedelta(days=1), interval='1d', progress=False)

# Get monthly data (last trading day of each month)
wti_monthly = wti.resample('M').last()
brent_monthly = brent.resample('M').last()

# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_monthly.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_monthly['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_monthly['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get current date and calculate proper historical range
today = datetime.now()
print(f"Today: {today}")

# Get the last 12 complete calendar months (going back from last month)
# If today is 2025-09-24, we want 2024-09 through 2025-08
current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
end_date = last_month_end

print(f"Adjusted analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data with wider range to ensure we get monthly data
fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

print(f"Fetching data from: {fetch_start.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {fetch_end.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data
wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

print(f"Raw WTI data shape: {wti.shape}")
print(f"Raw Brent data shape: {brent.shape}")

if not wti.empty and not brent.empty:
    print(f"WTI date range: {wti.index.min()} to {wti.index.max()}")
    print(f"Brent date range: {brent.index.min()} to {brent.index.max()}")
    
    # Get monthly data (last trading day of each month)
    wti_monthly = wti.resample('M').last()
    brent_monthly = brent.resample('M').last()
    
    print(f"Monthly WTI data shape: {wti_monthly.shape}")
    print(f"Monthly Brent data shape: {brent_monthly.shape}")
    
    # Filter to our target period
    mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
    wti_monthly = wti_monthly[mask]
    brent_monthly = brent_monthly[mask]
    
    print(f"Filtered monthly data shapes - WTI: {wti_monthly.shape}, Brent: {brent_monthly.shape}")
    
    print("\nWTI Monthly Close Prices:")
    print(wti_monthly[['Close']])
    
    print("\nBrent Monthly Close Prices:")
    print(brent_monthly[['Close']])
else:
    print("No data retrieved!")
```

```python 
# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_monthly.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_monthly['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_monthly['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get current date and calculate proper historical range
today = datetime.now()
current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
end_date = last_month_end

print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data with wider range to ensure we get monthly data
fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

# Fetch data
wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

# Get monthly data (last trading day of each month)
wti_monthly = wti.resample('M').last()
brent_monthly = brent.resample('M').last()

# Filter to our target period
mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
wti_monthly = wti_monthly[mask]
brent_monthly = brent_monthly[mask]

# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_monthly.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_monthly['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_monthly['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")
```

```python 
import yfinance as yf

# Fetch data with wider range
fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

brent_monthly = brent.resample('M').last()
```

```python 
# Now create the proper analysis with the correct data access
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_filtered.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_filtered['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_filtered['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")

# Show signals generated
signals_generated = df[df['Signal'] != 'Flat']
print(f"\nSignals generated: {len(signals_generated)}")
if len(signals_generated) > 0:
    print(signals_generated[['Month', 'Signal', 'Z_Score_6m', 'Spread']])
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get current date and calculate proper historical range
today = datetime.now()
current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
end_date = last_month_end

print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data with wider range
fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

# Get monthly data
wti_monthly = wti.resample('ME').last()  # Use 'ME' instead of deprecated 'M'
brent_monthly = brent.resample('ME').last()

# Filter to target period
mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
wti_filtered = wti_monthly[mask]
brent_filtered = brent_monthly[mask]

# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = wti_filtered.index.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_filtered['Close'].round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_filtered['Close'].round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")

# Show signals generated
signals_generated = df[df['Signal'] != 'Flat']
print(f"\nSignals generated: {len(signals_generated)}")
if len(signals_generated) > 0:
    print("Signals:")
    print(signals_generated[['Month', 'Signal', 'Z_Score_6m', 'Spread']].to_string(index=False))
```

<svg width="14px" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M13.0164 2C10.8193 2 9.03825 3.72453 9.03825 5.85185V8.51852H15.9235V9.25926H5.97814C3.78107 9.25926 2 10.9838 2 13.1111L2 18.8889C2 21.0162 3.78107 22.7407 5.97814 22.7407H8.27322V19.4815C8.27322 17.3542 10.0543 15.6296 12.2514 15.6296H19.5956C21.4547 15.6296 22.9617 14.1704 22.9617 12.3704V5.85185C22.9617 3.72453 21.1807 2 18.9836 2H13.0164ZM12.0984 6.74074C12.8589 6.74074 13.4754 6.14378 13.4754 5.40741C13.4754 4.67103 12.8589 4.07407 12.0984 4.07407C11.3378 4.07407 10.7213 4.67103 10.7213 5.40741C10.7213 6.14378 11.3378 6.74074 12.0984 6.74074Z" fill="#327EBD"/><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M18.9834 30C21.1805 30 22.9616 28.2755 22.9616 26.1482V23.4815L16.0763 23.4815L16.0763 22.7408L26.0217 22.7408C28.2188 22.7408 29.9998 21.0162 29.9998 18.8889V13.1111C29.9998 10.9838 28.2188 9.25928 26.0217 9.25928L23.7266 9.25928V12.5185C23.7266 14.6459 21.9455 16.3704 19.7485 16.3704L12.4042 16.3704C10.5451 16.3704 9.03809 17.8296 9.03809 19.6296L9.03809 26.1482C9.03809 28.2755 10.8192 30 13.0162 30H18.9834ZM19.9015 25.2593C19.1409 25.2593 18.5244 25.8562 18.5244 26.5926C18.5244 27.329 19.1409 27.9259 19.9015 27.9259C20.662 27.9259 21.2785 27.329 21.2785 26.5926C21.2785 25.8562 20.662 25.2593 19.9015 25.2593Z" fill="#FFDA4B"/></svg> `python-execute`

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def get_oil_data_and_analysis():
    # Get current date and calculate proper historical range
    today = datetime.now()
    current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
    last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
    start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
    end_date = last_month_end

    print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

    # Fetch data with wider range
    fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
    fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

    wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
    brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

    # Get monthly data
    wti_monthly = wti.resample('ME').last()  
    brent_monthly = brent.resample('ME').last()

    # Filter to target period
    mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
    wti_filtered = wti_monthly[mask]
    brent_filtered = brent_monthly[mask]

    print(f"Data shapes after filtering: WTI {wti_filtered.shape}, Brent {brent_filtered.shape}")
    
    # Check column structure
    print("WTI columns:", wti_filtered.columns.tolist())
    print("Brent columns:", brent_filtered.columns.tolist())
    
    # Access the Close prices correctly
    if wti_filtered.columns.nlevels > 1:
        # Multi-level columns
        wti_close = wti_filtered[('Close', 'CL=F')]
        brent_close = brent_filtered[('Close', 'BZ=F')]
    else:
        # Single level columns
        wti_close = wti_filtered['Close']
        brent_close = brent_filtered['Close']
    
    print(f"WTI close prices: {wti_close.values}")
    print(f"Brent close prices: {brent_close.values}")
    
    return wti_close, brent_close, wti_filtered.index

# Run the function
wti_close, brent_close, dates = get_oil_data_and_analysis()
```
</div>

<div className="result-box">
üîç`tool result`
<Accordion title="full return">
```json
=== STDOUT ===
Analysis period: 2024-09-01 to 2025-08-31
```

```python 
# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = dates.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_close.round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_close.round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("Oil Market Analysis Summary:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")

# Show signals generated
signals_generated = df[df['Signal'] != 'Flat']
print(f"\nSignals generated: {len(signals_generated)}")
if len(signals_generated) > 0:
    print("Signals:")
    print(signals_generated[['Month', 'Signal', 'Z_Score_6m', 'Spread']].to_string(index=False))
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

# Get current date and calculate proper historical range
today = datetime.now()
current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
end_date = last_month_end

print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

# Fetch data with wider range
fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

# Get monthly data
wti_monthly = wti.resample('ME').last()  
brent_monthly = brent.resample('ME').last()

# Filter to target period
mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
wti_filtered = wti_monthly[mask]
brent_filtered = brent_monthly[mask]

# Access the Close prices correctly (multi-level columns)
wti_close = wti_filtered[('Close', 'CL=F')]
brent_close = brent_filtered[('Close', 'BZ=F')]
dates = wti_filtered.index

# Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
df = pd.DataFrame()
df['Month'] = dates.strftime('%Y-%m')
df['WTI_Close'] = wti_close.round(4)
df['Brent_Close'] = brent_close.round(4)

# Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

# Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

# Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
    z_scores = []
    for i in range(len(series)):
        if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
            z_scores.append(0.0)
        else:
            # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
            window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
            if len(window_data) < 4:
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                mean = window_data.mean()
                std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                if std == 0:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                    # Clip to [-3, 3]
                    z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                    z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
    return z_scores

df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

# Generate trading signals based on z-score
def generate_signal(z_score):
    if z_score <= -1:
        return "Long Spread"
    elif z_score >= 1:
        return "Short Spread"
    else:
        return "Flat"

df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

# Determine regime based on z-score
def determine_regime(z_score):
    if z_score >= 1:
        return "High"
    elif z_score <= -1:
        return "Low"
    else:
        return "Neutral"

df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("OIL MARKET ANALYSIS SUMMARY")
print("="*80)
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Save for later use
oil_market_data = df.copy()
print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")

# Show signals generated
signals_generated = df[df['Signal'] != 'Flat']
print(f"\nSignals generated: {len(signals_generated)}")
if len(signals_generated) > 0:
    print("\nTRADING SIGNALS:")
    print(signals_generated[['Month', 'Signal', 'Z_Score_6m', 'Spread']].to_string(index=False))
```

```text workspace/oil_analysis.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def main():
    # Get current date and calculate proper historical range
    today = datetime.now()
    current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
    last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
    start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
    end_date = last_month_end

    print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

    # Fetch data with wider range
    fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
    fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

    wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
    brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

    # Get monthly data
    wti_monthly = wti.resample('ME').last()  
    brent_monthly = brent.resample('ME').last()

    # Filter to target period
    mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
    wti_filtered = wti_monthly[mask]
    brent_filtered = brent_monthly[mask]

    # Access the Close prices correctly (multi-level columns)
    wti_close = wti_filtered[('Close', 'CL=F')]
    brent_close = brent_filtered[('Close', 'BZ=F')]
    dates = wti_filtered.index

    # Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
    df = pd.DataFrame()
    df['Month'] = dates.strftime('%Y-%m')
    df['WTI_Close'] = wti_close.values.round(4)
    df['Brent_Close'] = brent_close.values.round(4)

    # Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
    df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

    # Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
    df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
    df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
    df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

    # Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
    def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
        z_scores = []
        for i in range(len(series)):
            if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
                window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
                if len(window_data) < 4:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    mean = window_data.mean()
                    std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                    if std == 0:
                        z_scores.append(0.0)
                    else:
                        z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                        # Clip to [-3, 3]
                        z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                        z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
        return z_scores

    df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

    # Generate trading signals based on z-score
    def generate_signal(z_score):
        if z_score <= -1:
            return "Long Spread"
        elif z_score >= 1:
            return "Short Spread"
        else:
            return "Flat"

    df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

    # Determine regime based on z-score
    def determine_regime(z_score):
        if z_score >= 1:
            return "High"
        elif z_score <= -1:
            return "Low"
        else:
            return "Neutral"

    df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

    print("\n" + "="*80)
    print("OIL MARKET ANALYSIS SUMMARY")
    print("="*80)
    print(df.to_string(index=False))

    print(f"\nTotal months analyzed: {len(df)}")
    print(f"Spread range: {df['Spread'].min():.4f} to {df['Spread'].max():.4f}")
    print(f"Z-Score range: {df['Z_Score_6m'].min():.4f} to {df['Z_Score_6m'].max():.4f}")

    # Show signals generated
    signals_generated = df[df['Signal'] != 'Flat']
    print(f"\nSignals generated: {len(signals_generated)}")
    if len(signals_generated) > 0:
        print("\nTRADING SIGNALS:")
        print(signals_generated[['Month', 'Signal', 'Z_Score_6m', 'Spread']].to_string(index=False))

    return df, wti_close, brent_close, dates

if __name__ == "__main__":
    oil_market_data, wti_close, brent_close, dates = main()
```

```python 
# Now implement the backtest strategy
def implement_backtest(df):
    """
    Implement the z-score based spread trading strategy backtest
    """
    trades = []
    
    # Iterate through the data to generate trades
    for i in range(len(df) - 1):  # -1 because we need next month for exit
        current_signal = df.iloc[i]['Signal']
        
        if current_signal != 'Flat':
            entry_month = df.iloc[i]['Month']
            exit_month = df.iloc[i + 1]['Month']
            entry_spread = df.iloc[i]['Spread']
            exit_spread = df.iloc[i + 1]['Spread']
            entry_wti = df.iloc[i]['WTI_Close']
            entry_brent = df.iloc[i]['Brent_Close']
            exit_wti = df.iloc[i + 1]['WTI_Close']
            exit_brent = df.iloc[i + 1]['Brent_Close']
            
            # Calculate individual leg returns
            wti_return = (exit_wti / entry_wti - 1) * 100
            brent_return = (exit_brent / entry_brent - 1) * 100
            
            # Calculate spread return based on signal
            if current_signal == "Long Spread":
                # Long Brent, Short WTI
                gross_return = (brent_return - wti_return) / 2  # Equal weight
                leg_returns = f"Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%, WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%"
            else:  # Short Spread
                # Short Brent, Long WTI
                gross_return = (wti_return - brent_return) / 2  # Equal weight
                leg_returns = f"WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%, Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%"
            
            # Apply 0.40% round-trip cost
            net_return = gross_return - 0.40
            
            trades.append({
                'Entry Month': entry_month,
                'Exit Month': exit_month,
                'Signal': current_signal,
                'Entry Spread': entry_spread,
                'Exit Spread': exit_spread,
                'Leg Returns %': leg_returns,
                'Gross PnL %': round(gross_return, 2),
                'Net PnL %': round(net_return, 2),
                'Notes': f"Z-Score: {df.iloc[i]['Z_Score_6m']:.4f}"
            })
    
    return trades

# Run the backtest
trades = implement_backtest(oil_market_data)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("SPREAD TRADING STRATEGY BACKTEST")
print("="*80)

if trades:
    trades_df = pd.DataFrame(trades)
    print("\nTRADE DETAILS:")
    print(trades_df.to_string(index=False))
    
    # Calculate performance metrics
    net_returns = [trade['Net PnL %'] for trade in trades]
    total_return = sum(net_returns)
    num_trades = len(trades)
    
    # Annualized return (assuming monthly trades over 12 months)
    annualized_return = total_return * (12 / num_trades) if num_trades > 0 else 0
    
    # Win rate
    winning_trades = [r for r in net_returns if r > 0]
    win_rate = (len(winning_trades) / num_trades * 100) if num_trades > 0 else 0
    
    # Sharpe ratio (simplified - using returns std dev)
    if len(net_returns) > 1:
        returns_std = np.std(net_returns, ddof=1)
        sharpe_ratio = (np.mean(net_returns) / returns_std * np.sqrt(12)) if returns_std > 0 else 0
    else:
        sharpe_ratio = 0
    
    # Maximum drawdown
    cumulative_returns = np.cumsum(net_returns)
    running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cumulative_returns)
    drawdown = cumulative_returns - running_max
    max_drawdown = abs(min(drawdown)) if len(drawdown) > 0 else 0
    
    print(f"\n" + "="*50)
    print("PERFORMANCE SUMMARY")
    print("="*50)
    print(f"Period: {oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[0]} to {oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[-1]}")
    print(f"Total Trades: {num_trades}")
    print(f"Total Return: {total_return:.2f}%")
    print(f"Annualized Return: {annualized_return:.2f}%")
    print(f"Sharpe Ratio (ann.): {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")
    print(f"Win Rate: {win_rate:.2f}%")
    print(f"Max Drawdown: {max_drawdown:.2f}%")
    print(f"Cost Assumption: 0.40% round-trip")
    
    # Store metrics for Notion update
    backtest_metrics = {
        'Period Start': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[0],
        'Period End': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[-1],
        'Trades': num_trades,
        'Total Return %': round(total_return, 2),
        'Annualized Return %': round(annualized_return, 2),
        'Sharpe (ann.)': round(sharpe_ratio, 2),
        'Win Rate %': round(win_rate, 2),
        'Max Drawdown %': round(max_drawdown, 2),
        'Cost Assumption': '0.40% round-trip'
    }
    
else:
    print("No trades executed in the backtest period.")
    backtest_metrics = {
        'Period Start': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[0],
        'Period End': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[-1],
        'Trades': 0,
        'Total Return %': 0.0,
        'Annualized Return %': 0.0,
        'Sharpe (ann.)': 0.0,
        'Win Rate %': 0.0,
        'Max Drawdown %': 0.0,
        'Cost Assumption': '0.40% round-trip'
    }
```

```python 
# Now implement the backtest strategy
def implement_backtest(df):
    """
    Implement the z-score based spread trading strategy backtest
    """
    trades = []
    
    # Iterate through the data to generate trades
    for i in range(len(df) - 1):  # -1 because we need next month for exit
        current_signal = df.iloc[i]['Signal']
        
        if current_signal != 'Flat':
            entry_month = df.iloc[i]['Month']
            exit_month = df.iloc[i + 1]['Month']
            entry_spread = df.iloc[i]['Spread']
            exit_spread = df.iloc[i + 1]['Spread']
            entry_wti = df.iloc[i]['WTI_Close']
            entry_brent = df.iloc[i]['Brent_Close']
            exit_wti = df.iloc[i + 1]['WTI_Close']
            exit_brent = df.iloc[i + 1]['Brent_Close']
            
            # Calculate individual leg returns
            wti_return = (exit_wti / entry_wti - 1) * 100
            brent_return = (exit_brent / entry_brent - 1) * 100
            
            # Calculate spread return based on signal
            if current_signal == "Long Spread":
                # Long Brent, Short WTI
                gross_return = (brent_return - wti_return) / 2  # Equal weight
                leg_returns = f"Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%, WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%"
            else:  # Short Spread
                # Short Brent, Long WTI
                gross_return = (wti_return - brent_return) / 2  # Equal weight
                leg_returns = f"WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%, Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%"
            
            # Apply 0.40% round-trip cost
            net_return = gross_return - 0.40
            
            trades.append({
                'Entry Month': entry_month,
                'Exit Month': exit_month,
                'Signal': current_signal,
                'Entry Spread': entry_spread,
                'Exit Spread': exit_spread,
                'Leg Returns %': leg_returns,

                'Net PnL %': round(net_return, 2),
                'Notes': f"Z-Score: {df.iloc[i]['Z_Score_6m']:.4f}"
            })
    
    return trades
```

```python 
# Create the data to update Notion databases
# First, let's prepare the data for Oil Market Summary

# Delete the existing empty record and create new ones
import json

print("Preparing data for Notion updates...")

# Oil Market Summary data
oil_market_summary_data = []
for _, row in oil_market_data.iterrows():
    oil_market_summary_data.append({
        'Month': row['Month'],
        'WTI_Close': row['WTI_Close'],
        'Brent_Close': row['Brent_Close'],
        'Spread': row['Spread'],
        'WTI_MoM': row['WTI_MoM'] if not pd.isna(row['WTI_MoM']) else None,
        'Brent_MoM': row['Brent_MoM'] if not pd.isna(row['Brent_MoM']) else None,
        'Spread_MoM': row['Spread_MoM'] if not pd.isna(row['Spread_MoM']) else None,
        'Z_Score_6m': row['Z_Score_6m'],
        'Signal': row['Signal'],
        'Regime': row['Regime']
    })

print("Oil Market Summary data prepared:")
for i, data in enumerate(oil_market_summary_data[:3]):  # Show first 3
    print(f"  {i+1}. {data['Month']}: WTI={data['WTI_Close']}, Brent={data['Brent_Close']}, Spread={data['Spread']}, Signal={data['Signal']}")

print(f"  ... and {len(oil_market_summary_data)-3} more records")

# Backtest data

for key, value in backtest_metrics.items():

for i, trade in enumerate(trades):
    print(f"  Trade {i+1}: {trade['Entry Month']} -> {trade['Exit Month']}, {trade['Signal']}, Net PnL: {trade['Net PnL %']}%")
```

```python 
# Run the complete analysis and prepare Notion updates
exec(open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/oil_analysis.py').read())

# Implement backtest
def implement_backtest(df):
    trades = []
    for i in range(len(df) - 1):
        current_signal = df.iloc[i]['Signal']
        if current_signal != 'Flat':
            entry_month = df.iloc[i]['Month']
            exit_month = df.iloc[i + 1]['Month']
            entry_spread = df.iloc[i]['Spread']
            exit_spread = df.iloc[i + 1]['Spread']
            entry_wti = df.iloc[i]['WTI_Close']
            entry_brent = df.iloc[i]['Brent_Close']
            exit_wti = df.iloc[i + 1]['WTI_Close']
            exit_brent = df.iloc[i + 1]['Brent_Close']
            
            wti_return = (exit_wti / entry_wti - 1) * 100
            brent_return = (exit_brent / entry_brent - 1) * 100
            
            if current_signal == "Long Spread":
                gross_return = (brent_return - wti_return) / 2
                leg_returns = f"Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%, WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%"
            else:
                gross_return = (wti_return - brent_return) / 2
                leg_returns = f"WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%, Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%"
            
            net_return = gross_return - 0.40
            
            trades.append({
                'Entry Month': entry_month,
                'Exit Month': exit_month,
                'Signal': current_signal,
                'Entry Spread': entry_spread,
                'Exit Spread': exit_spread,
                'Leg Returns %': leg_returns,
                'Net PnL %': round(net_return, 2),
                'Notes': f"Z-Score: {df.iloc[i]['Z_Score_6m']:.4f}"
            })
    return trades

trades = implement_backtest(oil_market_data)

# Calculate metrics
net_returns = [trade['Net PnL %'] for trade in trades]
total_return = sum(net_returns)
num_trades = len(trades)
annualized_return = total_return * (12 / num_trades) if num_trades > 0 else 0
winning_trades = [r for r in net_returns if r > 0]
win_rate = (len(winning_trades) / num_trades * 100) if num_trades > 0 else 0

if len(net_returns) > 1:
    returns_std = np.std(net_returns, ddof=1)
    sharpe_ratio = (np.mean(net_returns) / returns_std * np.sqrt(12)) if returns_std > 0 else 0
else:
    sharpe_ratio = 0

cumulative_returns = np.cumsum(net_returns)
running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cumulative_returns)
drawdown = cumulative_returns - running_max
max_drawdown = abs(min(drawdown)) if len(drawdown) > 0 else 0

backtest_metrics = {
    'Period Start': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[0],
    'Period End': oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[-1],
    'Trades': num_trades,
    'Total Return %': round(total_return, 2),
    'Annualized Return %': round(annualized_return, 2),
    'Sharpe (ann.)': round(sharpe_ratio, 2),
    'Win Rate %': round(win_rate, 2),
    'Max Drawdown %': round(max_drawdown, 2),
    'Cost Assumption': '0.40% round-trip'
}

print("Data preparation complete!")
print(f"Oil market data: {len(oil_market_data)} months")
print(f"Backtest trades: {len(trades)}")
print(f"Performance: {total_return:.2f}% total return, {win_rate:.1f}% win rate")
```

```text workspace/update_notion.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import yfinance as yf
from dateutil.relativedelta import relativedelta
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def get_oil_data_and_analysis():
    # Get current date and calculate proper historical range
    today = datetime.now()
    current_month_start = today.replace(day=1)
    last_month_end = current_month_start - timedelta(days=1)
    start_date = (last_month_end.replace(day=1) - relativedelta(months=11))
    end_date = last_month_end

    print(f"Analysis period: {start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

    # Fetch data
    fetch_start = start_date - timedelta(days=5)
    fetch_end = end_date + timedelta(days=5)

    wti = yf.download('CL=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)
    brent = yf.download('BZ=F', start=fetch_start, end=fetch_end, interval='1d', progress=False)

    # Get monthly data
    wti_monthly = wti.resample('ME').last()  
    brent_monthly = brent.resample('ME').last()

    # Filter to target period
    mask = (wti_monthly.index >= start_date) & (wti_monthly.index <= end_date)
    wti_filtered = wti_monthly[mask]
    brent_filtered = brent_monthly[mask]

    # Access the Close prices correctly
    wti_close = wti_filtered[('Close', 'CL=F')]
    brent_close = brent_filtered[('Close', 'BZ=F')]
    dates = wti_filtered.index

    # Create comprehensive analysis dataframe
    df = pd.DataFrame()
    df['Month'] = dates.strftime('%Y-%m')
    df['WTI_Close'] = wti_close.values.round(4)
    df['Brent_Close'] = brent_close.values.round(4)

    # Calculate Brent-WTI Spread
    df['Spread'] = (df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']).round(4)

    # Calculate Month-over-Month percentages
    df['WTI_MoM'] = ((df['WTI_Close'] / df['WTI_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
    df['Brent_MoM'] = ((df['Brent_Close'] / df['Brent_Close'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)
    df['Spread_MoM'] = ((df['Spread'] / df['Spread'].shift(1) - 1) * 100).round(2)

    # Calculate Z-Score (6-month rolling)
    def calculate_zscore(series, window=6):
        z_scores = []
        for i in range(len(series)):
            if i < 3:  # Less than 4 samples
                z_scores.append(0.0)
            else:
                # Get last 6 values (or available values if less than 6)
                window_data = series.iloc[max(0, i-5):i+1]
                if len(window_data) < 4:
                    z_scores.append(0.0)
                else:
                    mean = window_data.mean()
                    std = window_data.std(ddof=1)  # Sample standard deviation
                    if std == 0:
                        z_scores.append(0.0)
                    else:
                        z_score = (series.iloc[i] - mean) / std
                        # Clip to [-3, 3]
                        z_score = np.clip(z_score, -3, 3)
                        z_scores.append(round(z_score, 4))
        return z_scores

    df['Z_Score_6m'] = calculate_zscore(df['Spread'])

    # Generate trading signals based on z-score
    def generate_signal(z_score):
        if z_score <= -1:
            return "Long Spread"
        elif z_score >= 1:
            return "Short Spread"
        else:
            return "Flat"

    df['Signal'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(generate_signal)

    # Determine regime based on z-score
    def determine_regime(z_score):
        if z_score >= 1:
            return "High"
        elif z_score <= -1:
            return "Low"
        else:
            return "Neutral"

    df['Regime'] = df['Z_Score_6m'].apply(determine_regime)

    return df

def implement_backtest(df):
    trades = []
    for i in range(len(df) - 1):
        current_signal = df.iloc[i]['Signal']
        if current_signal != 'Flat':
            entry_month = df.iloc[i]['Month']
            exit_month = df.iloc[i + 1]['Month']
            entry_spread = df.iloc[i]['Spread']
            exit_spread = df.iloc[i + 1]['Spread']
            entry_wti = df.iloc[i]['WTI_Close']
            entry_brent = df.iloc[i]['Brent_Close']
            exit_wti = df.iloc[i + 1]['WTI_Close']
            exit_brent = df.iloc[i + 1]['Brent_Close']
            
            wti_return = (exit_wti / entry_wti - 1) * 100
            brent_return = (exit_brent / entry_brent - 1) * 100
            
            if current_signal == "Long Spread":
                gross_return = (brent_return - wti_return) / 2
                leg_returns = f"Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%, WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%"
            else:
                gross_return = (wti_return - brent_return) / 2
                leg_returns = f"WTI: {wti_return:.2f}%, Brent: {brent_return:.2f}%"
            
            net_return = gross_return - 0.40
            
            trades.append({
                'Entry Month': entry_month,
                'Exit Month': exit_month,
                'Signal': current_signal,
                'Entry Spread': entry_spread,
                'Exit Spread': exit_spread,
                'Leg Returns %': leg_returns,
                'Net PnL %': round(net_return, 2),
                'Notes': f"Z-Score: {df.iloc[i]['Z_Score_6m']:.4f}"
            })
    return trades

def calculate_backtest_metrics(trades):
    net_returns = [trade['Net PnL %'] for trade in trades]
    total_return = sum(net_returns)
    num_trades = len(trades)
    annualized_return = total_return * (12 / num_trades) if num_trades > 0 else 0
    winning_trades = [r for r in net_returns if r > 0]
    win_rate = (len(winning_trades) / num_trades * 100) if num_trades > 0 else 0

    if len(net_returns) > 1:
        returns_std = np.std(net_returns, ddof=1)
        sharpe_ratio = (np.mean(net_returns) / returns_std * np.sqrt(12)) if returns_std > 0 else 0
    else:
        sharpe_ratio = 0

    cumulative_returns = np.cumsum(net_returns)
    running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cumulative_returns)
    drawdown = cumulative_returns - running_max
    max_drawdown = abs(min(drawdown)) if len(drawdown) > 0 else 0

    return {
        'Total Return %': round(total_return, 2),
        'Annualized Return %': round(annualized_return, 2),
        'Sharpe (ann.)': round(sharpe_ratio, 2),
        'Win Rate %': round(win_rate, 2),
        'Max Drawdown %': round(max_drawdown, 2),
        'Trades': num_trades
    }

def main():
    print("Starting Oil Price Analysis and Notion Update...")
    
    # Get analysis data
    oil_market_data = get_oil_data_and_analysis()
    
    # Run backtest
    trades = implement_backtest(oil_market_data)
    backtest_metrics = calculate_backtest_metrics(trades)
    
    print(f"\nAnalysis Complete:")
    print(f"- Oil market data: {len(oil_market_data)} months")
    print(f"- Trading signals: {len(oil_market_data[oil_market_data['Signal'] != 'Flat'])}")
    print(f"- Backtest trades: {len(trades)}")
    print(f"- Total return: {backtest_metrics['Total Return %']}%")
    print(f"- Win rate: {backtest_metrics['Win Rate %']}%")
    
    return oil_market_data, trades, backtest_metrics

if __name__ == "__main__":
    oil_market_data, trades, backtest_metrics = main()
```

```python 
# Now let's create records for Oil Market Summary
print("\nCreating Oil Market Summary records...")

# Create records for each month
for i, (_, row) in enumerate(oil_market_data.iterrows()):
    if i >= 3:  # Let's create just the first 3 records for now
        break
        
    month_str = row['Month']
    print(f"\nMonth {month_str}:")
    print(f"  WTI: ${row['WTI_Close']:.4f}")
    print(f"  Brent: ${row['Brent_Close']:.4f}")
    print(f"  Spread: ${row['Spread']:.4f}")
    print(f"  Z-Score: {row['Z_Score_6m']:.4f}")
    print(f"  Signal: {row['Signal']}")
    print(f"  Regime: {row['Regime']}")
    
    # Handle NaN values for MoM percentages
    wti_mom = None if pd.isna(row['WTI_MoM']) else row['WTI_MoM']
    brent_mom = None if pd.isna(row['Brent_MoM']) else row['Brent_MoM']
    spread_mom = None if pd.isna(row['Spread_MoM']) else row['Spread_MoM']
    
    print(f"  MoM: WTI={wti_mom}, Brent={brent_mom}, Spread={spread_mom}")

print(f"\nBacktest Summary:")
print(f"Period: {oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[0]} to {oil_market_data['Month'].iloc[-1]}")
print(f"Trades: {backtest_metrics['Trades']}")
print(f"Total Return: {backtest_metrics['Total Return %']}%")
print(f"Annualized Return: {backtest_metrics['Annualized Return %']}%")
print(f"Sharpe Ratio: {backtest_metrics['Sharpe (ann.)']}")
print(f"Win Rate: {backtest_metrics['Win Rate %']}%")
print(f"Max Drawdown: {backtest_metrics['Max Drawdown %']}%")

print(f"\nTrades executed:")
for i, trade in enumerate(trades):
    print(f"  {i+1}. {trade['Entry Month']} -> {trade['Exit Month']}: {trade['Signal']}, Net PnL: {trade['Net PnL %']}%")
```

```text workspace/oil_analysis_summary.md
# Oil Price Analysis and Z-Score Spread Trading Strategy Report

## Executive Summary

This report presents a comprehensive analysis of WTI and Brent crude oil prices over the last 12 months (September 2024 - August 2025) and implements a z-score-based spread trading strategy backtest.

## Data Analysis Period
- **Start Date**: 2024-09-01
- **End Date**: 2025-08-31
- **Data Source**: Yahoo Finance (WTI: CL=F, Brent: BZ=F)
- **Frequency**: Monthly (last trading day of each month)

## Key Market Insights

### Price Movements
- **WTI Price Range**: $58.21 - $72.53 (24.6% range)
- **Brent Price Range**: $63.12 - $76.76 (21.6% range)
- **Spread Range**: $2.50 - $4.94 (97.6% range)

### Notable Events
1. **April 2025**: Significant oil price decline (-18.56% WTI, -15.55% Brent)
2. **December 2024**: Spread compression to $2.92 (lowest level)
3. **April 2025**: Spread widening to $4.91 (highest level)

### Spread Analysis
- **Average Spread**: $3.55
- **Spread Volatility**: High, with MoM changes ranging from -40.89% to +50.61%
- **Z-Score Range**: -1.2447 to +1.1053

## Trading Strategy Performance

### Strategy Rules
- **Long Spread Signal**: Z-Score ‚â§ -1 (Long Brent, Short WTI)
- **Short Spread Signal**: Z-Score ‚â• +1 (Short Brent, Long WTI)
- **Flat Position**: -1 < Z-Score < +1
- **Position Duration**: 1 month (entry at month-end, exit at next month-end)
- **Cost**: 0.40% round-trip transaction cost

### Performance Metrics
- **Total Return**: 1.71%
- **Annualized Return**: 6.84%
- **Sharpe Ratio**: 3.39
- **Win Rate**: 100% (3/3 trades profitable)
- **Maximum Drawdown**: 0.00%
- **Number of Trades**: 3

### Trade Details

#### Trade 1: December 2024 Long Spread
- **Entry**: 2024-12, Spread = $2.92, Z-Score = -1.0950
- **Exit**: 2025-01, Spread = $4.23
- **Position**: Long Brent (+2.84%), Short WTI (+1.13%)
- **Net P&L**: +0.46%

#### Trade 2: April 2025 Short Spread
- **Entry**: 2025-04, Spread = $4.91, Z-Score = +1.1053
- **Exit**: 2025-05, Spread = $3.11
- **Position**: Short Brent (+1.24%), Long WTI (+4.43%)
- **Net P&L**: +1.20%

#### Trade 3: June 2025 Long Spread
- **Entry**: 2025-06, Spread = $2.50, Z-Score = -1.2447
- **Exit**: 2025-07, Spread = $3.27
- **Position**: Long Brent (+7.28%), Short WTI (+6.37%)
- **Net P&L**: +0.05%

## Risk Analysis

### Strategy Strengths
1. **Perfect Win Rate**: All trades were profitable
2. **Strong Risk-Adjusted Returns**: Sharpe ratio of 3.39 indicates excellent risk-adjusted performance
3. **Mean Reversion**: Strategy successfully captured spread mean reversion
4. **No Drawdowns**: Zero maximum drawdown during the period

### Strategy Limitations
1. **Limited Sample Size**: Only 3 trades over 12 months
2. **Market Regime Dependency**: Performance may vary in different market conditions
3. **Transaction Costs**: 0.40% round-trip cost significantly impacts smaller profits
4. **Timing Risk**: Monthly rebalancing may miss intra-month opportunities

## Technical Implementation

### Z-Score Calculation
- **Window**: 6-month rolling window
- **Method**: Sample standard deviation (ddof=1)
- **Clipping**: Values clipped to [-3, +3] range
- **Threshold**: Minimum 4 samples required for calculation

### Data Quality
- **Precision**: Prices rounded to 4 decimal places
- **Percentages**: MoM changes rounded to 2 decimal places
- **Missing Data**: Handled appropriately for first months

## Conclusion

The z-score-based spread trading strategy demonstrated strong performance during the analyzed period, achieving:
- Positive returns in all executed trades
- Strong risk-adjusted performance (Sharpe ratio: 3.39)
- Effective capture of spread mean reversion opportunities

However, the strategy's performance is based on a limited sample size and specific market conditions. Future implementation should consider:
- Longer backtesting periods
- Different market regimes
- Alternative signal thresholds
- Dynamic position sizing

## Data Sources and Methodology

- **Data Provider**: Yahoo Finance API
- **Analysis Tools**: Python (pandas, numpy, yfinance)
- **Storage**: Notion databases (Oil Market Summary, Spread Strategy Backtest)
- **Calculation Standards**: As per technical specifications in detail.md

*Analysis period: September 2024 - August 2025*
```

```json
- **Data**: Fetch monthly data for WTI (CL=F) and Brent (BZ=F) from Yahoo Finance for the last 12 complete calendar months. Prices should be rounded to 4 decimal places, percentages to 2 decimal places.
- **Calculations**:

  | Indicator        | Description                                                                                                                                |
  | ---------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
  | Brent-WTI Spread | Brent Close - WTI Close                                                                                                                    |
  | MoM%             | (Current Month / Previous Month - 1) √ó 100%                                                                                                |
  | Z-Score(6m)      | Standardized using mean and SAMPLE standard deviation (ddof=1) of the last 6 spreads (z=0 when sample < 4 or std = 0, clipped to [-3,3]).  |

- **Backtest Strategy**: Generate signals based on z-score (z ‚â§ -1: long spread = long Brent + short WTI; z ‚â• +1: short spread = short Brent + long WTI; otherwise flat). Signals generated at month-end, held for 1 month, closed at next month-end. Only one position at a time; equal weight for both legs; 0.40% round-trip cost included in monthly net returns. Calculate total return, annualized return, Sharpe ratio, win rate, and maximum drawdown.

  - **Tip:** Entry Month refers to signal generation month, Exit Month refers to position closing month. Position returns are calculated from signal generation month to position closing month (spanning 2 calendar months)

- **Write results to** **`Oil Market Summary`** **Oil Market Summary** and **`Spread Strategy Backtest`** **Spread Strategy Backtest** data tables. For `Spread Strategy Backtest`, update the unique "Metric" row and add/update corresponding "Trade" rows for each executed trade:

  - When Type=Metric: fill in `Period Start`, `Period End`, `Trades`, `Total Return %`, `Annualized Return %`, `Sharpe (ann.)`, `Win Rate %`, `Max Drawdown %`, `Cost Assumption`;
  - When Type=Trade: fill in `Entry Month`, `Exit Month`, `Signal`, `Entry Spread`, `Exit Spread`, `Leg Returns %`, `Net PnL %`, `Notes`.
```

```python oil_market_analysis.py

import pandas as pd

wti_data = [{"Date":"2024-10-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":68.4100036621,"High":78.4599990845,"Low":66.3300018311,"Close":69.2600021362,"Volume":7647098,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2024-11-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":70.4400024414,"High":72.8799972534,"Low":66.6100006104,"Close":68.0,"Volume":5980019,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-01-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":71.8499984741,"High":80.7699966431,"Low":71.7900009155,"Close":72.5299987793,"Volume":6940780,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-02-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":74.1399993896,"High":75.1800003052,"Low":68.3600006104,"Close":69.7600021362,"Volume":5320902,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-03-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":69.9499969482,"High":71.8300018311,"Low":65.2200012207,"Close":71.4800033569,"Volume":5307703,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-04-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":71.3899993896,"High":72.2799987793,"Low":55.1199989319,"Close":58.2099990845,"Volume":7119077,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-05-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":58.1599998474,"High":64.1900024414,"Low":55.2999992371,"Close":60.7900009155,"Volume":5761820,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-07-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":64.9599990845,"High":70.5100021362,"Low":64.6699981689,"Close":69.2600021362,"Volume":5083485,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-08-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":69.3499984741,"High":69.5800018311,"Low":61.9399986267,"Close":64.0100021362,"Volume":4912110,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-09-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":63.9500007629,"High":66.0299987793,"Low":61.4500007629,"Close":62.4000015259,"Volume":3289481,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0}]
brent_data = [{"Date":"2024-10-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":72.0,"High":82.0800018311,"Low":69.9100036621,"Close":73.1600036621,"Volume":952900,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2024-11-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":74.1299972534,"High":76.2300033569,"Low":70.6999969482,"Close":72.9400024414,"Volume":684173,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-01-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":74.8799972534,"High":82.6299972534,"Low":74.7300033569,"Close":76.7600021362,"Volume":1055033,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-02-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":76.8199996948,"High":77.5299987793,"Low":72.3899993896,"Close":73.1800003052,"Volume":714183,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-03-01T05:00:00.000Z","Open":73.0699996948,"High":74.7900009155,"Low":68.3399963379,"Close":74.7399978638,"Volume":726527,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-04-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":74.6299972534,"High":75.4599990845,"Low":58.3899993896,"Close":63.1199989319,"Volume":1306864,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-05-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":61.1399993896,"High":67.4899978638,"Low":58.4099998474,"Close":63.9000015259,"Volume":1032061,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-07-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":66.5899963379,"High":73.6299972534,"Low":66.3399963379,"Close":72.5299987793,"Volume":903089,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-08-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":71.7699966431,"High":71.9899978638,"Low":65.0,"Close":68.1200027466,"Volume":721891,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0},{"Date":"2025-09-01T04:00:00.000Z","Open":67.4300003052,"High":69.5100021362,"Low":65.0800018311,"Close":66.6800003052,"Volume":555800,"Dividends":0.0,"Stock Splits":0.0}]

wti_df = pd.DataFrame(wti_data)
brent_df = pd.DataFrame(brent_data)

wti_df['Date'] = pd.to_datetime(wti_df['Date'])
brent_df['Date'] = pd.to_datetime(brent_df['Date'])

wti_df = wti_df.rename(columns={'Close': 'WTI_Close'})
brent_df = brent_df.rename(columns={'Close': 'Brent_Close'})

df = pd.merge(wti_df[['Date', 'WTI_Close']], brent_df[['Date', 'Brent_Close']], on='Date')

df['Brent-WTI Spread'] = df['Brent_Close'] - df['WTI_Close']
df['WTI_MoM%'] = (df['WTI_Close'].pct_change() * 100).round(2)
df['Brent_MoM%'] = (df['Brent_Close'].pct_change() * 100).round(2)


def calculate_z_score(series):
    if len(series) < 4:
        return 0
    mean = series.mean()
    std = series.std(ddof=1)
    if std == 0:
        return 0
    z_score = (series.iloc[-1] - mean) / std
    return max(min(z_score, 3), -3)

df['Z-Score(6m)'] = df['Brent-WTI Spread'].rolling(window=6).apply(calculate_z_score, raw=False)


def backtest(df):
    df['Signal'] = 0
    df.loc[df['Z-Score(6m)'] <= -1, 'Signal'] = 1
    df.loc[df['Z-Score(6m)'] >= 1, 'Signal'] = -1

    df['Position'] = df['Signal'].shift(1)
    df['Position'].fillna(0, inplace=True)

    df['Brent_Return'] = df['Brent_Close'].pct_change()
    df['WTI_Return'] = df['WTI_Close'].pct_change()

    df['Strategy_Return'] = 0.0
    df.loc[df['Position'] == 1, 'Strategy_Return'] = df['Brent_Return'] - df['WTI_Return']
    df.loc[df['Position'] == -1, 'Strategy_Return'] = df['WTI_Return'] - df['Brent_Return']

    cost = 0.0040
    df['Trade_Cost'] = 0
    df.loc[df['Position'] != df['Position'].shift(1), 'Trade_Cost'] = cost

    df['Net_Return'] = df['Strategy_Return'] - df['Trade_Cost']

    total_return = (1 + df['Net_Return']).prod() - 1
    annualized_return = (1 + total_return)**(12 / len(df)) - 1
    annualized_volatility = df['Net_Return'].std() * (12**0.5)
    sharpe_ratio = annualized_return / annualized_volatility if annualized_volatility != 0 else 0
    
    trades = df[df['Position'] != 0]
    win_rate = (trades['Net_Return'] > 0).sum() / len(trades) if len(trades) > 0 else 0

    cumulative_return = (1 + df['Net_Return']).cumprod()
    peak = cumulative_return.expanding(min_periods=1).max()
    drawdown = (cumulative_return - peak) / peak
    max_drawdown = drawdown.min()
    
    backtest_results = {
        "total_return": total_return,
        "annualized_return": annualized_return,
        "sharpe_ratio": sharpe_ratio,
        "win_rate": win_rate,
        "max_drawdown": max_drawdown,
        "trades": len(trades)
    }

    return backtest_results, df

backtest_metrics, backtest_df = backtest(df.copy())

print("--- Oil Market Summary ---")
print(df.round(4).to_string())

print("\n--- Spread Strategy Backtest ---")
print(backtest_df.round(4).to_string())

print("\n--- Backtest Metrics ---")
print(backtest_metrics)

```
</div>
